# Demo "Observing indirect subprocessed with apt-get"
This is a script that updates the system using apt-get. It observes all subprocesses recursively, even though they are not shells.
## Script
```sh
export OTEL_SHELL_CONFIG_OBSERVE_SUBPROCESSES=TRUE
. otel.sh
sudo apt-get update
```
## Trace Structure Overview
```
bash -e demo.sh
  sudo apt-get update
    apt-get update
      /usr/bin/dpkg --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --print-foreign-architectures
      /usr/lib/apt/methods/https
      /usr/lib/apt/methods/mirror+file
      apt-get update
        sh -c -- [ ! -e /run/systemd/system ] || [ $(id -u) -ne 0 ] || systemctl start --no-block apt-news.service esm-cache.service >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
          id -u
          systemctl start --no-block apt-news.service esm-cache.service
      /usr/lib/apt/methods/file
      /usr/lib/apt/methods/http
      /usr/lib/apt/methods/gpgv
      /usr/lib/apt/methods/store
      /usr/lib/apt/methods/store
      /usr/lib/apt/methods/gpgv
        /usr/lib/apt/methods/gpgv
          /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
            /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
            apt-config shell MASTER_KEYRING APT::Key::MasterKeyring
              /usr/bin/dpkg --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --print-foreign-architectures
            apt-config shell ARCHIVE_KEYRING APT::Key::ArchiveKeyring
              /usr/bin/dpkg --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --print-foreign-architectures
            apt-config shell REMOVED_KEYS APT::Key::RemovedKeys
              /usr/bin/dpkg --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --print-foreign-architectures
            apt-config shell ARCHIVE_KEYRING_URI APT::Key::ArchiveKeyringURI
              /usr/bin/dpkg --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --print-foreign-architectures
            /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
            apt-config shell GPGV Apt::Key::gpgvcommand ASSERT_PUBKEY_ALGO Apt::Key::assert-pubkey-algo
              /usr/bin/dpkg --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --force-confdef --force-confold --print-foreign-architectures
            /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
              gpgv --assert-pubkey-algo
            mktemp --directory --tmpdir apt-key-gpghome.XXXXXXXXXX
            chmod 700 /tmp/apt-key-gpghome.53FOvsgok2
            /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
            /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
              /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
              sed -e s#'#'\"'\"'#g
            /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
              /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
              sed -e s#'#'\"'\"'#g
            /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
            gpgv --assert-pubkey-algo=>=rsa1024,ed25519,ed448,nistp256,nistp384,nistp512,brainpoolP256r1,brainpoolP320r1,brainpoolP384r1,brainpoolP512r1,secp256k1 --homedir /tmp/apt-key-gpghome.53FOvsgok2 --keyring /etc/apt/keyrings/microsoft.gpg --ignore-time-conflict --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.Wi1fQ9 /tmp/apt.data.N1IXzR
            gpgconf --kill all
              gpg-connect-agent --homedir /tmp/apt-key-gpghome.53FOvsgok2 --no-autostart --dirmngr KILLDIRMNGR
              gpg-connect-agent --homedir /tmp/apt-key-gpghome.53FOvsgok2 -s --no-autostart GETINFO scd_running /if ${! $?} scd killscd /end
              gpg-connect-agent --homedir /tmp/apt-key-gpghome.53FOvsgok2 --no-autostart KILLAGENT
              gpg-connect-agent --no-autostart --keyboxd KILLKEYBOXD --homedir /tmp/apt-key-gpghome.53FOvsgok2
            rm -rf /tmp/apt-key-gpghome.53FOvsgok2
        /usr/lib/apt/methods/gpgv
          /usr/bin/apt-key --quiet --readonly --keyring /usr/share/keyrings/ubuntu-archive-keyring.gpg verify --status-fd 3 /tmp/apt.sig.EK6YUb /tmp/apt.data.18r9KL
```
